## Accessibility

European Accessibility Act (EAA), EN 301 549, EU Web Accessibility Directive, and accessibility conformance testing.

- [ACT Rules](https://github.com/act-rules/act-rules.github.io) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/act-rules/act-rules.github.io?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/act-rules/act-rules.github.io/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/act-rules/act-rules.github.io?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/act-rules/act-rules.github.io/commits/develop) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/act-rules/act-rules.github.io?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/act-rules/act-rules.github.io) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/act-rules/act-rules.github.io?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/act-rules/act-rules.github.io/blob/develop/LICENSE.md) [![EAA](https://img.shields.io/badge/EAA-003399?style=flat-square)](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/eli/dir/2019/882/oj) [![EN301549](https://img.shields.io/badge/EN301549-003399?style=flat-square)](https://www.etsi.org/deliver/etsi_en/301500_301599/301549/) - Community-maintained accessibility conformance testing rules used to harmonize EU EN 301 549 compliance evaluation.
- [Alfa](https://github.com/Siteimprove/alfa) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Siteimprove/alfa?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/Siteimprove/alfa/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/Siteimprove/alfa?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/Siteimprove/alfa/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/Siteimprove/alfa?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/Siteimprove/alfa) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/Siteimprove/alfa?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/Siteimprove/alfa/blob/main/LICENSE.md) [![EAA](https://img.shields.io/badge/EAA-003399?style=flat-square)](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/eli/dir/2019/882/oj) [![EN301549](https://img.shields.io/badge/EN301549-003399?style=flat-square)](https://www.etsi.org/deliver/etsi_en/301500_301599/301549/) - Standards-based accessibility conformance testing suite implementing ACT Rules for EN 301 549 and WCAG.
- [BIK Web Test](https://github.com/BIK-BITV/BIK-Web-Test) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/BIK-BITV/BIK-Web-Test?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/BIK-BITV/BIK-Web-Test/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/BIK-BITV/BIK-Web-Test?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/BIK-BITV/BIK-Web-Test/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/BIK-BITV/BIK-Web-Test?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/BIK-BITV/BIK-Web-Test) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/BIK-BITV/BIK-Web-Test?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/BIK-BITV/BIK-Web-Test) [![EAA](https://img.shields.io/badge/EAA-003399?style=flat-square)](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/eli/dir/2019/882/oj) [![EN301549](https://img.shields.io/badge/EN301549-003399?style=flat-square)](https://www.etsi.org/deliver/etsi_en/301500_301599/301549/) - Test procedures for evaluating web accessibility against WCAG 2.1 and EN 301 549 criteria.
- [RAAM](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteMobile) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteMobile?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteMobile/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteMobile?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteMobile/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteMobile?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteMobile) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteMobile?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteMobile/blob/main/LICENSE.md) [![EAA](https://img.shields.io/badge/EAA-003399?style=flat-square)](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/eli/dir/2019/882/oj) [![EN301549](https://img.shields.io/badge/EN301549-003399?style=flat-square)](https://www.etsi.org/deliver/etsi_en/301500_301599/301549/) - Mobile app accessibility assessment framework covering all EN 301 549 criteria.
- [RAWEB](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteWeb) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteWeb?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteWeb/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteWeb?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteWeb/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteWeb?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteWeb) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteWeb?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/ReferentielAccessibiliteWeb) [![EAA](https://img.shields.io/badge/EAA-003399?style=flat-square)](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/eli/dir/2019/882/oj) [![EN301549](https://img.shields.io/badge/EN301549-003399?style=flat-square)](https://www.etsi.org/deliver/etsi_en/301500_301599/301549/) - Web accessibility assessment framework covering all EN 301 549 criteria for website evaluation.
- [SimplA11yMonit](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yMonit) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yMonit?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yMonit/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yMonit?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yMonit/commits/master) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yMonit?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yMonit) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yMonit?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yMonit/blob/master/LICENSE) [![EAA](https://img.shields.io/badge/EAA-003399?style=flat-square)](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/eli/dir/2019/882/oj) - Tool implementing the EU simplified accessibility monitoring method from Commission Decision 2018/1524.
- [SimplA11yPDFCrawler](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yPDFCrawler) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yPDFCrawler?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yPDFCrawler/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yPDFCrawler?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yPDFCrawler/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yPDFCrawler?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yPDFCrawler) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yPDFCrawler?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/accessibility-luxembourg/simplA11yPDFCrawler/blob/main/LICENSE) [![EAA](https://img.shields.io/badge/EAA-003399?style=flat-square)](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/eli/dir/2019/882/oj) - Crawler that downloads PDFs from websites and analyses their accessibility against EU standards.

## Agriculture and Food Safety

EFSA, Common Agricultural Policy (CAP), RASFF, EU food labeling, and pan-European agricultural data.

- [EFSA Catalogue Browser](https://github.com/openefsa/catalogue-browser) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/openefsa/catalogue-browser?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/openefsa/catalogue-browser/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/openefsa/catalogue-browser?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openefsa/catalogue-browser/commits/master) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/openefsa/catalogue-browser?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openefsa/catalogue-browser) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/openefsa/catalogue-browser?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openefsa/catalogue-browser/blob/master/LICENSE) - Java application for browsing EFSA food safety catalogues and FoodEx2 classifications.
- [JRC Checks by Monitoring](https://github.com/ec-jrc/cbm) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ec-jrc/cbm?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/ec-jrc/cbm/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ec-jrc/cbm?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/ec-jrc/cbm/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/ec-jrc/cbm?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/ec-jrc/cbm) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/ec-jrc/cbm?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/ec-jrc/cbm/blob/main/LICENSE) [![CAP](https://img.shields.io/badge/CAP-003399?style=flat-square)](https://agriculture.ec.europa.eu/common-agricultural-policy_en) [![Copernicus](https://img.shields.io/badge/Copernicus-003399?style=flat-square)](https://www.copernicus.eu/) - JRC toolkit for CAP area-based checks by monitoring using Copernicus Sentinel data.
- [Nutri-Score Calculator](https://github.com/food-nutrients/nutri-score) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/food-nutrients/nutri-score?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/food-nutrients/nutri-score/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/food-nutrients/nutri-score?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/food-nutrients/nutri-score/commits/master) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/food-nutrients/nutri-score?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/food-nutrients/nutri-score) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/food-nutrients/nutri-score?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/food-nutrients/nutri-score) [![FIC](https://img.shields.io/badge/FIC-003399?style=flat-square)](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/eli/reg/2011/1169/oj) - Library for calculating EU Nutri-Score food nutrition labels.
- [Open Food Facts Folksonomy](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/folksonomy_api) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/openfoodfacts/folksonomy_api?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/folksonomy_api/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/openfoodfacts/folksonomy_api?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/folksonomy_api/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/openfoodfacts/folksonomy_api?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/folksonomy_api) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/openfoodfacts/folksonomy_api?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/folksonomy_api/blob/main/LICENSE) - REST API for the Open Food Facts folksonomy engine for tagging food products.
- [Open Food Facts Mobile](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/smooth-app) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/openfoodfacts/smooth-app?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/smooth-app/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/openfoodfacts/smooth-app?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/smooth-app/commits/develop) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/openfoodfacts/smooth-app?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/smooth-app) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/openfoodfacts/smooth-app?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/smooth-app/blob/develop/LICENSE) [![FIC](https://img.shields.io/badge/FIC-003399?style=flat-square)](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/eli/reg/2011/1169/oj) - Mobile application for scanning and contributing to the food products database with EU Nutri-Score support.
- [Open Food Facts Python](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-python) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-python?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-python/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-python?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-python/commits/develop) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-python?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-python) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-python?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-python/blob/develop/LICENSE) [![FIC](https://img.shields.io/badge/FIC-003399?style=flat-square)](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/eli/reg/2011/1169/oj) - Python package for accessing the Open Food Facts database including EU Nutri-Score and food labeling data.
- [Open Food Facts Server](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-server) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-server?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-server/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-server?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-server/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-server?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-server) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-server?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/openfoodfacts-server/blob/main/LICENSE) - Database, API and web interface for the collaborative food products database with EU nutrition labeling support.
- [Robotoff](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/robotoff) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/openfoodfacts/robotoff?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/robotoff/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/openfoodfacts/robotoff?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/robotoff/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/openfoodfacts/robotoff?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/robotoff) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/openfoodfacts/robotoff?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openfoodfacts/robotoff/blob/main/LICENCE) - Machine learning prediction service for Open Food Facts product categorization and quality checks.
- [Sen4CAP](https://github.com/Sen4CAP/Sen4CAP) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Sen4CAP/Sen4CAP?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/Sen4CAP/Sen4CAP/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/Sen4CAP/Sen4CAP?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/Sen4CAP/Sen4CAP/commits/master) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/Sen4CAP/Sen4CAP?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/Sen4CAP/Sen4CAP) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/Sen4CAP/Sen4CAP?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/Sen4CAP/Sen4CAP/blob/master/LICENSE.txt) [![CAP](https://img.shields.io/badge/CAP-003399?style=flat-square)](https://agriculture.ec.europa.eu/common-agricultural-policy_en) [![Copernicus](https://img.shields.io/badge/Copernicus-003399?style=flat-square)](https://www.copernicus.eu/) - ESA-funded Sentinels for Common Agricultural Policy monitoring system.

## Anti-Money Laundering and Compliance

EU Anti-Money Laundering Directives (AMLD), sanctions screening, KYC/KYB, beneficial ownership, and LEI tools.

- [Beneficial Ownership Data Standard](https://github.com/openownership/data-standard) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/openownership/data-standard?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/openownership/data-standard/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/openownership/data-standard?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openownership/data-standard/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/openownership/data-standard?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openownership/data-standard) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/openownership/data-standard?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openownership/data-standard/blob/main/LICENSE) [![AMLD](https://img.shields.io/badge/AMLD-003399?style=flat-square)](https://finance.ec.europa.eu/financial-crime/anti-money-laundering-and-countering-financing-terrorism_en) - Open standard for publishing beneficial ownership data, aligned with EU AMLD transparency requirements.
- [Follow the Money](https://github.com/alephdata/followthemoney) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alephdata/followthemoney?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/alephdata/followthemoney/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/alephdata/followthemoney?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/alephdata/followthemoney/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/alephdata/followthemoney?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/alephdata/followthemoney) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/alephdata/followthemoney?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/alephdata/followthemoney/blob/main/LICENSE) [![AMLD](https://img.shields.io/badge/AMLD-003399?style=flat-square)](https://finance.ec.europa.eu/financial-crime/anti-money-laundering-and-countering-financing-terrorism_en) - Data model and processing tools for investigative entity data used in EU AML compliance.
- [Memorious](https://github.com/alephdata/memorious) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alephdata/memorious?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/alephdata/memorious/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/alephdata/memorious?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/alephdata/memorious/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/alephdata/memorious?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/alephdata/memorious) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/alephdata/memorious?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/alephdata/memorious/blob/main/LICENSE) [![AMLD](https://img.shields.io/badge/AMLD-003399?style=flat-square)](https://finance.ec.europa.eu/financial-crime/anti-money-laundering-and-countering-financing-terrorism_en) - Lightweight web scraping toolkit for documents and structured data used in investigative compliance.
- [Nomenklatura](https://github.com/opensanctions/nomenklatura) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/opensanctions/nomenklatura?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/opensanctions/nomenklatura/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/opensanctions/nomenklatura?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/opensanctions/nomenklatura/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/opensanctions/nomenklatura?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/opensanctions/nomenklatura) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/opensanctions/nomenklatura?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/opensanctions/nomenklatura/blob/main/LICENSE) [![AMLD](https://img.shields.io/badge/AMLD-003399?style=flat-square)](https://finance.ec.europa.eu/financial-crime/anti-money-laundering-and-countering-financing-terrorism_en) - Framework for integrating FollowTheMoney entity data from multiple sources for EU AML compliance.
- [OpenAleph](https://github.com/openaleph/openaleph) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/openaleph/openaleph?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/openaleph/openaleph/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/openaleph/openaleph?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openaleph/openaleph/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/openaleph/openaleph?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openaleph/openaleph) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/openaleph/openaleph?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/openaleph/openaleph/blob/main/LICENSE.txt) [![AMLD](https://img.shields.io/badge/AMLD-003399?style=flat-square)](https://finance.ec.europa.eu/financial-crime/anti-money-laundering-and-countering-financing-terrorism_en) - Open source investigative data platform for securely cross-referencing datasets using the FollowTheMoney schema.
- [OpenSanctions](https://github.com/opensanctions/opensanctions) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/opensanctions/opensanctions?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/opensanctions/opensanctions/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/opensanctions/opensanctions?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/opensanctions/opensanctions/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/opensanctions/opensanctions?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/opensanctions/opensanctions) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/opensanctions/opensanctions?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/opensanctions/opensanctions/blob/main/LICENSE) [![AMLD](https://img.shields.io/badge/AMLD-003399?style=flat-square)](https://finance.ec.europa.eu/financial-crime/anti-money-laundering-and-countering-financing-terrorism_en) - Open database of international sanctions data, persons of interest and politically exposed persons, including EU sanctions lists.
- [pygleif](https://github.com/ggravlingen/pygleif) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ggravlingen/pygleif?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/ggravlingen/pygleif/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ggravlingen/pygleif?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/ggravlingen/pygleif/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/ggravlingen/pygleif?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/ggravlingen/pygleif) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/ggravlingen/pygleif?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/ggravlingen/pygleif/blob/main/LICENSE) [![AMLD](https://img.shields.io/badge/AMLD-003399?style=flat-square)](https://finance.ec.europa.eu/financial-crime/anti-money-laundering-and-countering-financing-terrorism_en) - Python client for the GLEIF Legal Entity Identifier API used in EU regulatory compliance.
- [Yente](https://github.com/opensanctions/yente) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/opensanctions/yente?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/opensanctions/yente/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/opensanctions/yente?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/opensanctions/yente/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/opensanctions/yente?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/opensanctions/yente) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/opensanctions/yente?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/opensanctions/yente/blob/main/LICENSE) [![AMLD](https://img.shields.io/badge/AMLD-003399?style=flat-square)](https://finance.ec.europa.eu/financial-crime/anti-money-laundering-and-countering-financing-terrorism_en) - Entity matching and search API for OpenSanctions data, supporting EU sanctions screening and KYC workflows.

## Central Banking and Monetary Policy

ECB APIs, TARGET2/T2S/TIPS, Euribor/ESTR, euro exchange rates, and Eurosystem tools.

- [CurrencyConverter](https://github.com/alexprengere/currencyconverter) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alexprengere/currencyconverter?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/alexprengere/currencyconverter/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/alexprengere/currencyconverter?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/alexprengere/currencyconverter/commits/master) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/alexprengere/currencyconverter?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/alexprengere/currencyconverter) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/alexprengere/currencyconverter?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/alexprengere/currencyconverter/blob/master/LICENSE) - Python currency converter using historical exchange rate data from the European Central Bank.
- [ecb](https://github.com/expersso/ecb) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/expersso/ecb?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/expersso/ecb/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/expersso/ecb?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/expersso/ecb/commits/master) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/expersso/ecb?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/expersso/ecb) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/expersso/ecb?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/expersso/ecb) - R interface to the European Central Bank Statistical Data Warehouse API.
- [eu_central_bank](https://github.com/RubyMoney/eu_central_bank) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RubyMoney/eu_central_bank?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/RubyMoney/eu_central_bank/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/RubyMoney/eu_central_bank?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/RubyMoney/eu_central_bank/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/RubyMoney/eu_central_bank?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/RubyMoney/eu_central_bank) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/RubyMoney/eu_central_bank?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/RubyMoney/eu_central_bank/blob/main/LICENSE) - Ruby gem that calculates exchange rates using published rates from the European Central Bank.
- [Euribor](https://github.com/datasets/euribor) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/datasets/euribor?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/datasets/euribor/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/datasets/euribor?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/datasets/euribor/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/datasets/euribor?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/datasets/euribor) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/datasets/euribor?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/datasets/euribor) - Open dataset of Euribor rates by year and granularity.
- [Frankfurter](https://github.com/lineofflight/frankfurter) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lineofflight/frankfurter?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/lineofflight/frankfurter/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/lineofflight/frankfurter?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/lineofflight/frankfurter/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/lineofflight/frankfurter?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/lineofflight/frankfurter) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/lineofflight/frankfurter?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/lineofflight/frankfurter/blob/main/LICENSE) - Currency data API built on top of ECB exchange rates.

## Democracy and Governance

European Parliament, EU elections, Transparency Register, European Citizens' Initiative, and EU legislative tracking.

## eIDAS and Digital Identity

Electronic Identification, Authentication and Trust Services regulation for cross-border digital identity, including the EU Digital Identity Wallet.

- [AltMe Wallet](https://github.com/TalaoDAO/AltMe) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/TalaoDAO/AltMe?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/TalaoDAO/AltMe/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/TalaoDAO/AltMe?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/TalaoDAO/AltMe/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/TalaoDAO/AltMe?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/TalaoDAO/AltMe) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/TalaoDAO/AltMe?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/TalaoDAO/AltMe/blob/main/LICENSE) [![eIDAS](https://img.shields.io/badge/eIDAS-003399?style=flat-square)](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/eli/reg/2014/910/oj) - Open source Self Sovereign Identity wallet with EBSI conformance and EUDI wallet ARF implementation.

## Electronic Invoicing

Peppol, EN 16931, and the EU e-invoicing directive (2014/55/EU) for cross-border electronic invoicing.

## Energy and Electricity

ENTSO-E Transparency Platform, ACER, REMIT, and the European energy market.

- [Spine Toolbox](https://github.com/spine-tools/Spine-Toolbox) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/spine-tools/Spine-Toolbox?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/spine-tools/Spine-Toolbox/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/spine-tools/Spine-Toolbox?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/spine-tools/Spine-Toolbox/commits/master) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/spine-tools/Spine-Toolbox?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/spine-tools/Spine-Toolbox) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/spine-tools/Spine-Toolbox?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/spine-tools/Spine-Toolbox/blob/master/COPYING) - EU-funded data and workflow management tool for energy system modelling and simulation.
- [SpineOpt](https://github.com/spine-tools/SpineOpt.jl) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/spine-tools/SpineOpt.jl?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/spine-tools/SpineOpt.jl/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/spine-tools/SpineOpt.jl?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/spine-tools/SpineOpt.jl/commits/master) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/spine-tools/SpineOpt.jl?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/spine-tools/SpineOpt.jl) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/spine-tools/SpineOpt.jl?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/spine-tools/SpineOpt.jl/blob/master/LICENSE) - EU-funded adaptable modelling framework for multi-energy systems in Julia.
- [technology-data](https://github.com/PyPSA/technology-data) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PyPSA/technology-data?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/PyPSA/technology-data/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/PyPSA/technology-data?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/PyPSA/technology-data/commits/master) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/PyPSA/technology-data?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/PyPSA/technology-data) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/PyPSA/technology-data?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/PyPSA/technology-data/blob/master/LICENSE.txt) - Compiled assumptions on European energy system technologies including costs and efficiencies.

## European Utilities

Pan-European utility libraries: IBAN validation, NUTS regions, European phone numbers, postal codes, holidays, and locale tools.

- [date-holidays](https://github.com/commenthol/date-holidays) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/commenthol/date-holidays?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/commenthol/date-holidays/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/commenthol/date-holidays?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/commenthol/date-holidays/commits/master) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/commenthol/date-holidays?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/commenthol/date-holidays) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/commenthol/date-holidays?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/commenthol/date-holidays/blob/master/LICENSE) - JavaScript library providing public holiday data for countries worldwide including all EU member states.

## Finance and Capital Markets

EBA, ESMA regulations, MiFID II, MiCA, DORA, EMIR, XBRL/iXBRL reporting, and European financial market infrastructure.

- [Arelle](https://github.com/Arelle/Arelle) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Arelle/Arelle?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/Arelle/Arelle/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/Arelle/Arelle?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/Arelle/Arelle/commits/master) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/Arelle/Arelle?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/Arelle/Arelle) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/Arelle/Arelle?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/Arelle/Arelle/blob/master/LICENSE.md) - Open source XBRL platform for European financial reporting including EBA and ESMA taxonomies.

- [Brel](https://github.com/BrelLibrary/brel) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/BrelLibrary/brel?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/BrelLibrary/brel/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/BrelLibrary/brel?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/BrelLibrary/brel/commits/main) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/BrelLibrary/brel?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/BrelLibrary/brel) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/BrelLibrary/brel?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/BrelLibrary/brel/blob/main/LICENSE) - Python library for reading XBRL reports used in EU ESEF financial filings.

## Open Data and Statistics

Eurostat, EU Open Data Portal, SDMX, NUTS regions, and pan-European statistical infrastructure.

- [CKAN](https://github.com/ckan/ckan) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ckan/ckan?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/ckan/ckan/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ckan/ckan?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/ckan/ckan/commits/master) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/ckan/ckan?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/ckan/ckan) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/ckan/ckan?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/ckan/ckan/blob/master/LICENSE.txt) [![Open Data](https://img.shields.io/badge/Open%20Data-003399?style=flat-square)](https://data.europa.eu/) ([Demo](https://demo.ckan.org)) - Open source data management system powering many European government open data portals.

## Payments and Banking

SEPA, PSD2, Open Banking, EBICS, and the Single Euro Payments Area infrastructure.

- [ebics-client-php](https://github.com/ebics-api/ebics-client-php) [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ebics-api/ebics-client-php?style=flat-square&label=⭐)](https://github.com/ebics-api/ebics-client-php/stargazers) [![Last Commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ebics-api/ebics-client-php?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/ebics-api/ebics-client-php/commits/3.x) [![Language](https://img.shields.io/github/languages/top/ebics-api/ebics-client-php?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/ebics-api/ebics-client-php) [![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/ebics-api/ebics-client-php?style=flat-square)](https://github.com/ebics-api/ebics-client-php/blob/3.x/LICENSE) [![EBICS](https://img.shields.io/badge/EBICS-003399?style=flat-square)](https://www.ebics.org/) [![PSD2](https://img.shields.io/badge/PSD2-003399?style=flat-square)](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/eli/dir/2015/2366/oj) - PHP EBICS library supporting versions 2.4, 2.5, and 3.0 for European banking communication.

## Contributing

Contributions are welcome. Read the [contributing guidelines](contributing.md) before submitting a pull request.

## Footnotes

**Badge:** If your project is listed here, you can add one of these badges to your README:

![listed on awesome-europe](https://img.shields.io/badge/listed%20on-awesome--europe-ffcc00?style=flat&logo=europeanunion&logoColor=ffcc00&labelColor=003399) ![listed on awesome-europe](https://img.shields.io/badge/listed%20on-awesome--europe-ffcc00?style=flat-square&logo=europeanunion&logoColor=ffcc00&labelColor=003399) ![listed on awesome-europe](https://img.shields.io/badge/listed%20on-awesome--europe-ffcc00?style=plastic&logo=europeanunion&logoColor=ffcc00&labelColor=003399) ![listed on awesome-europe](https://img.shields.io/badge/listed%20on-awesome--europe-ffcc00?style=for-the-badge&logo=europeanunion&logoColor=ffcc00&labelColor=003399)

```markdown
[![listed on awesome-europe](https://img.shields.io/badge/listed%20on-awesome--europe-ffcc00?style=flat&logo=europeanunion&logoColor=ffcc00&labelColor=003399)](https://github.com/GeiserX/awesome-europe#readme)
```

For the badge (large):
```markdown
[![listed on awesome-europe](https://img.shields.io/badge/listed%20on-awesome--europe-ffcc00?style=for-the-badge&logo=europeanunion&logoColor=ffcc00&labelColor=003399)](https://github.com/GeiserX/awesome-europe#readme)
```

**Note:** This list focuses on open source software that provides **support specifically for Europe** — its institutions, regulations, standards, and cross-border infrastructure. The scope covers the **EU-27 and EEA** (Norway, Iceland, Liechtenstein). Software specific to a single country belongs in country-specific awesome lists. Software that is global and merely happens to work in Europe is also out of scope.

**Disclaimer:** No projects related to pornography, NSFW content, gambling, religion, partisan politics, or any other controversial topic are accepted. This list aims to be a neutral and useful technical resource for the developer community.
